--- [Nelson, Adrienne Camille - Federal Judicial Center] ---
You are here Nelson, Adrienne Camille Born 1967 in Kansas City, MO Federal Judicial Service: Judge, U.S. District Court for the District of Oregon Nominated by Joseph R. Biden on January 3, 2023, to a seat vacated by Michael W. Mosman. Confirmed by the Senate on February 15, 2023, and received commission on February 23, 2023. Education: University of Arkansas, B.A., 1989 University of Texas School of Law, J.D., 1993 Professional Career: Federal Judicial Service: Judge, U.S. District Court for the District of Oregon Nominated by Joseph R. Biden on January 3, 2023, to a seat vacated by Michael W. Mosman. Confirmed by the Senate on February 15, 2023, and received commission on February 23, 2023. Education: University of Arkansas, B.A., 1989 University of Texas School of Law, J.D., 1993 Professional Career: Attorney, Multnomah Defenders, Inc., Portland, Oregon, 1996-1999 Private practice, Portland, Oregon, 1999-2004 Adjunct professor, Lewis & Clark Law School, 2002-2005 Coordinator and senior attorney, Portland State University, 2004-2006 Judge, Oregon Circuit Court, Multnomah County, 2006-2018 Justice, Supreme Court of Oregon, 2018-2023 Nominated to U.S. District Court for the District of Oregon, July 14, 2022; no Senate vote


--- [Adrienne Nelson - Wikipedia] ---
Adrienne Camille Nelson (born 1967) is an American lawyer and jurist serving as a United States district judge of the United States District Court for the District of Oregon since 2023. She previously served as a justice of the Oregon Supreme Court from 2018 to 2023 and as a judge on the Multnomah County Circuit Court from 2006 to 2018.

--- [King Law - Law Office and Attorneys in Raleigh, North Carolina] ---
Wake County is home to King Law’s Raleigh office that offers legal services in the following practice areas: Alimony Assault & Battery Child Custody Child Support Cocaine Defense Collaborative Divorce Criminal Defense Divorce Divorce Mediation Domestic Violence Drug Crimes Drug Manufacturing Drug Possession Drug Trafficking DWI / DUI Elder law Equitable Distribution Estate law Family Law Felony Offenses Juvenile Crimes Mediation Misdemeanors Personal Injury Probation Violation Property Division Same Sex Divorce Sex Crimes Shoplifting Spousal Support Temporary Restraining Orders and Injunctions Theft Crimes Weapons Charges White Collar Crimes King Law opened in 2002 with its corporate office in Rutherfordton, North Carolina and since has expanded to include locations throughout western North Carolina, the upstate of South Carolina, and Eastern Tennesee. King Law expanded its office locations to Raleigh in January 2025 through a partnership with Heidgerd & Edwards, LLP, a well-established firm that has been serving Wake County since the 1970s. Raleigh attorneys and staff serve the general legal needs of the residents and tourists to the areas of Raleigh, Neuse, Cary, Knightdale, Garner, and other surrounding towns. Individuals facing legal dilemmas and in need of a lawyer in Wake County and surrounding counties should contact King Law at 919-861-2484 to schedule a consultation with a member of our legal team. Consultations are offered in-office, by telephone or virtually by Zoom. Our team of lawyers and legal professionals are ready to meet with you and take steps to achieve the best possible results for your legal need. How to Find the Office King Law’s Wake County office is in Raleigh located at 3737 Glenwood Ave #100, Raleigh, NC 27612. Raleigh Courthouse Information & City Resources 316 Fayetteville St, Raleigh, NC 27601 6716 Six Forks Rd, Raleigh, NC 27615
